## Overview

Linear algebra procedures useful for 3D spatial transformations.

## Types

### [Euler\_Angle\_Order ¶](#Euler_Angle_Order) [*Source*](https://github.com/odin-lang/Odin/tree/master/core/math/linalg/specific_euler_angles.odin#L3)

```
Euler_Angle_Order :: enum int {
	// Tait-Bryan
	XYZ, 
	XZY, 
	YXZ, 
	YZX, 
	ZXY, 
	ZYX, 
	// Proper Euler
	XYX, 
	XZX, 
	YXY, 
	YZY, 
	ZXZ, 
	ZYZ, 
}
```

The Data-Oriented Language for Sane Software Development.
